 Political Background: The Eulberia parliamentary constituency came into existence in the year 1952
 yah aisi sansadeey seat he jis par communiston ne bahut pehle hi dhamak de di thi
 In the elections of 1957, the Forward Bloc registered its presence here, while Congress mps were winning all over the country
 yah sansadeey kshetra haavda jile main aata he
 In 1952, Satyaban Rai of the Indian National Congress won from here
 saal 1957 main ethbm forward block(marxist)ke em ke aurbindaa ghoshaal vijayi hue
 In 1962, the Indian National Congress again occupied this seat and Punendu Khan was elected as an MP from here
 saal 1967 main indian neshnal congress ke je ke mandal ko safalataa mili lekin saal 1971 aate-aate sipiem ne yahaan par apni pakad majboot bana lee
 In 1971, Prasad Bhattacharya of CPM won the elections
 saal 1977 main bhi shyama prasanna bhattacharya ko safalataa mili
 Even in the year 1980, cpm's Hannan Mollah got success from here and till the years 1984, 1989, 1991, 1996, 1998 1999, 2000, the cpm's Hannan Mollah retained this seat but a change had come that earlier He used to fight the Indian National Congress but in 1999, the All India Trinamool Congress came into the fight
 saal 2004 main bhi ol india trinmul congress duusare number par thi
 In 2009, the game was overturned and Ahmad Sultan of All India Trinamool Congress defeated Hannan Mollah, who has been MP for several times
 hannan mollah saal 1980 se saal 2004 tak lagaataar saansad rahe the or unhen sipiem kaa kaddavar netaa mana jaataa tha
